"""Kimi-Linear W4A16 hybrid decode unit — fused int4 dequant-GEMV.

A from-scratch rewrite of reference.py that keeps the same module/state layout
and numerical recipe, but does every weight-bound projection as a fused
int4-unpack + per-group dequant + GEMV so the weights are streamed at int4
bandwidth and never materialized as bf16.
"""
from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass, field

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import torch.nn.functional as F
import triton
import triton.language as tl

OP_TYPE = "kimi_linear_w4a16_decode"
HARDWARE_REQUIRED = ["RTX_PRO_6000"]
EPS = 1.0e-6
GROUP_SIZE = 128


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class Config:
    hidden: int = 2304
    kda_heads: int = 32
    kda_head_dim: int = 128
    short_conv: int = 4
    mla_heads: int = 32
    kv_lora: int = 512
    qk_nope: int = 128
    qk_rope: int = 64
    v_head: int = 128
    rope_theta: float = 10000.0
    n_experts: int = 64
    n_active: int = 8
    n_shared: int = 1
    moe_inter: int = 1024
    routed_scaling: float = 2.446
    group: int = 128
    pattern: tuple = ("K", "K", "K", "M")
    dtype: torch.dtype = field(default=torch.bfloat16)


def build_config(shape: dict) -> Config:
    return Config(n_experts=int(shape.get("n_experts", 64)))


# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
# Fused int4 GEMV kernel
# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
@triton.autotune(
    configs=[
        triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 64}, num_warps=4, num_stages=1),
        triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 128}, num_warps=4, num_stages=1),
        triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 256}, num_warps=8, num_stages=1),
        triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 128}, num_warps=8, num_stages=1),
    ],
    key=["K", "N"],
)
@triton.jit
def int4_gemv_kernel(
    x_ptr,
    w_ptr,
    s_ptr,
    z_ptr,
    y_ptr,
    K,
    N,
    stride_wk,
    stride_wn,
    stride_sg,
    stride_sn,
    BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr,
):
    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    mask_n = offs_n < N

    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), dtype=tl.float32)

    num_blocks = (K + BLOCK_K - 1) // BLOCK_K
    for b in tl.range(0, num_blocks):
        k0 = b * BLOCK_K
        offs_kh = k0 // 2 + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K // 2)
        mask_kh = offs_kh < (K // 2)
        w_pack = tl.load(
            w_ptr + offs_kh[:, None] * stride_wk + offs_n[None, :] * stride_wn,
            mask=mask_kh[:, None] & mask_n[None, :],
            other=0,
        )
        lo = w_pack & 0xF
        hi = (w_pack >> 4) & 0xF
        w_u = tl.trans(tl.interleave(tl.trans(lo), tl.trans(hi)))

        g0 = k0 // 128
        scale = tl.load(
            s_ptr + g0 * stride_sg + offs_n * stride_sn,
            mask=mask_n,
            other=0.0,
        ).to(tl.float32)
        zero = tl.load(
            z_ptr + g0 * stride_sg + offs_n * stride_sn,
            mask=mask_n,
            other=0.0,
        ).to(tl.float32)

        w_f = (w_u.to(tl.float32) - zero) * scale

        offs_k = k0 + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
        mask_k = offs_k < K
        x = tl.load(x_ptr + offs_k, mask=mask_k, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)

        acc += tl.sum(w_f * x[:, None], axis=0)

    tl.store(y_ptr + offs_n, acc.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask_n)


def fused_int4_gemv(x: torch.Tensor, w_q: torch.Tensor, scales: torch.Tensor, zeros: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    """M=1 GEMV: x @ W, where W is int4 packed + group-128 asymmetric dequant.

    x:        [K] bf16 or fp16
    w_q:      [K//2, N] uint8
    scales:   [K//128, N] bf16
    zeros:    [K//128, N] bf16
    returns:  [N] bf16
    """
    assert x.dim() == 1
    K, N = w_q.shape[0] * 2, w_q.shape[1]
    y = torch.empty(N, dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
    def grid(meta):
        return (triton.cdiv(N, meta["BLOCK_N"]),)
    int4_gemv_kernel[grid](
        x,
        w_q,
        scales,
        zeros,
        y,
        K,
        N,
        w_q.stride(0),
        w_q.stride(1),
        scales.stride(0),
        scales.stride(1),
    )
    return y



@triton.autotune(
    configs=[
        triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 64}, num_warps=4, num_stages=1),
        triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 128}, num_warps=4, num_stages=1),
        triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 256}, num_warps=8, num_stages=1),
        triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 128}, num_warps=8, num_stages=1),
    ],
    key=["K", "N", "E"],
)
@triton.jit
def int4_gemv_batched_kernel(
    x_ptr,
    w_ptr,
    s_ptr,
    z_ptr,
    idx_ptr,
    y_ptr,
    K,
    N,
    E,
    stride_xe,
    stride_we,
    stride_wk,
    stride_wn,
    stride_se,
    stride_sg,
    stride_sn,
    stride_ye,
    stride_yn,
    BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr,
):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    e = tl.load(idx_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    mask_n = offs_n < N

    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), dtype=tl.float32)

    num_blocks = (K + BLOCK_K - 1) // BLOCK_K
    for b in tl.range(0, num_blocks):
        k0 = b * BLOCK_K
        offs_kh = k0 // 2 + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K // 2)
        mask_kh = offs_kh < (K // 2)
        w_pack = tl.load(
            w_ptr + e * stride_we + offs_kh[:, None] * stride_wk + offs_n[None, :] * stride_wn,
            mask=mask_kh[:, None] & mask_n[None, :],
            other=0,
        )
        lo = w_pack & 0xF
        hi = (w_pack >> 4) & 0xF
        w_u = tl.trans(tl.interleave(tl.trans(lo), tl.trans(hi)))

        g0 = k0 // 128
        scale = tl.load(
            s_ptr + e * stride_se + g0 * stride_sg + offs_n * stride_sn,
            mask=mask_n,
            other=0.0,
        ).to(tl.float32)
        zero = tl.load(
            z_ptr + e * stride_se + g0 * stride_sg + offs_n * stride_sn,
            mask=mask_n,
            other=0.0,
        ).to(tl.float32)

        w_f = (w_u.to(tl.float32) - zero) * scale

        offs_k = k0 + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
        mask_k = offs_k < K
        x = tl.load(x_ptr + pid_e * stride_xe + offs_k, mask=mask_k, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)

        acc += tl.sum(w_f * x[:, None], axis=0)

    tl.store(
        y_ptr + pid_e * stride_ye + offs_n * stride_yn,
        acc.to(tl.bfloat16),
        mask=mask_n,
    )


def fused_int4_gemv_batched(
    x: torch.Tensor,
    w_q: torch.Tensor,
    scales: torch.Tensor,
    zeros: torch.Tensor,
    idx: torch.Tensor,
) -> torch.Tensor:
    """Batched M=1 GEMV: for each selected expert i, compute x[i] @ W[idx[i]].

    x:        [K] or [E_sel, K] bf16
    w_q:      [E_total, K//2, N] uint8
    scales:   [E_total, K//128, N] bf16
    zeros:    [E_total, K//128, N] bf16
    idx:      [E_sel] int64 (indices into w_q/scales/zeros)
    returns:  [E_sel, N] bf16
    """
    E = idx.numel()
    if x.dim() == 1:
        x = x.unsqueeze(0).expand(E, -1).contiguous()
    assert x.dim() == 2 and x.shape[0] == E
    K = w_q.shape[1] * 2
    N = w_q.shape[2]
    y = torch.empty((E, N), dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
    def grid(meta):
        return (E, triton.cdiv(N, meta["BLOCK_N"]))
    int4_gemv_batched_kernel[grid](
        x,
        w_q,
        scales,
        zeros,
        idx,
        y,
        K,
        N,
        E,
        x.stride(0),
        w_q.stride(0),
        w_q.stride(1),
        w_q.stride(2),
        scales.stride(0),
        scales.stride(1),
        scales.stride(2),
        y.stride(0),
        y.stride(1),
    )
    return y


# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
# Quantization containers (same buffer names as reference.py)
# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
def _pack_int4(w_q: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    lo = w_q[0::2] & 0xF
    hi = w_q[1::2] & 0xF
    return (lo | (hi << 4)).contiguous()


def quantize(w_io: torch.Tensor, group: int = GROUP_SIZE):
    K, N = w_io.shape
    ng = K // group
    wg = w_io.view(ng, group, N).float()
    wmin = wg.min(dim=1, keepdim=True).values
    wmax = wg.max(dim=1, keepdim=True).values
    scales = (wmax - wmin).clamp_min(1e-8) / 15.0
    zeros = (-wmin / scales).round().clamp(0, 15)
    w_q = ((wg / scales) + zeros).round().clamp(0, 15).to(torch.uint8).view(K, N)
    return _pack_int4(w_q), scales.squeeze(1).to(torch.bfloat16), zeros.squeeze(1).to(torch.bfloat16)


def dequant(w_q: torch.Tensor, scales: torch.Tensor, zeros: torch.Tensor, K: int, group: int) -> torch.Tensor:
    """Reference dequant (only used for one-time cache warmup)."""
    wu = torch.empty((K, w_q.shape[1]), dtype=torch.uint8, device=w_q.device)
    wu[0::2] = w_q & 0xF
    wu[1::2] = (w_q >> 4) & 0xF
    s = scales.repeat_interleave(group, dim=0)[:K]
    z = zeros.repeat_interleave(group, dim=0)[:K]
    return (wu.to(torch.bfloat16) - z) * s


class QuantLinear(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, in_f: int, out_f: int, group: int = GROUP_SIZE):
        super().__init__()
        assert in_f % group == 0 and in_f % 2 == 0
        self.in_f, self.out_f, self.group = in_f, out_f, group
        ng = in_f // group
        self.register_buffer("w_q", torch.zeros(in_f // 2, out_f, dtype=torch.uint8))
        self.register_buffer("scales", torch.zeros(ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))
        self.register_buffer("zeros", torch.zeros(ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))

    def init_random(self, gen: torch.Generator, std: float = 0.02) -> None:
        w = torch.randn(self.in_f, self.out_f, generator=gen) * std
        wq, s, z = quantize(w, self.group)
        self.w_q.copy_(wq)
        self.scales.copy_(s)
        self.zeros.copy_(z)

    def forward(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
        return fused_int4_gemv(x, self.w_q, self.scales, self.zeros)


class QuantExperts(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, n: int, in_f: int, out_f: int, group: int = GROUP_SIZE):
        super().__init__()
        self.n, self.in_f, self.out_f, self.group = n, in_f, out_f, group
        ng = in_f // group
        self.register_buffer("w_q", torch.zeros(n, in_f // 2, out_f, dtype=torch.uint8))
        self.register_buffer("scales", torch.zeros(n, ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))
        self.register_buffer("zeros", torch.zeros(n, ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))

    def init_random(self, gen: torch.Generator, std: float = 0.02) -> None:
        for e in range(self.n):
            w = torch.randn(self.in_f, self.out_f, generator=gen) * std
            wq, s, z = quantize(w, self.group)
            self.w_q[e].copy_(wq)
            self.scales[e].copy_(s)
            self.zeros[e].copy_(z)

    def forward(self, e: int, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
        return fused_int4_gemv(x, self.w_q[e], self.scales[e], self.zeros[e])

    def forward_batched(self, x: torch.Tensor, idx: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
        return fused_int4_gemv_batched(x, self.w_q, self.scales, self.zeros, idx)


# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
# Helpers
# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
def _rmsnorm(x: torch.Tensor, w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    xf = x.float()
    xf = xf * torch.rsqrt(xf.pow(2).mean(-1, keepdim=True) + EPS)
    return (xf * w.float()).to(x.dtype)


def _rope_cossin(pos: int, dim: int, theta: float, device):
    inv = 1.0 / (theta ** (torch.arange(0, dim, 2, device=device, dtype=torch.float32) / dim))
    ang = pos * inv
    return torch.cos(ang), torch.sin(ang)


def _apply_rope(x: torch.Tensor, cos: torch.Tensor, sin: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    xf = x.float()
    even, odd = xf[..., 0::2], xf[..., 1::2]
    out = torch.empty_like(xf)
    out[..., 0::2] = even * cos - odd * sin
    out[..., 1::2] = odd * cos + even * sin
    return out.to(x.dtype)


# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
# Layers
# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
class KDA(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg: Config):
        super().__init__()
        self.cfg = cfg
        H, Dk, d = cfg.kda_heads, cfg.kda_head_dim, cfg.hidden
        self.q_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * Dk, cfg.group)
        self.k_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * Dk, cfg.group)
        self.v_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * Dk, cfg.group)
        self.g_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * Dk, cfg.group)
        self.beta_proj = nn.Linear(d, H, bias=False, dtype=cfg.dtype)
        self.conv_w = nn.Parameter(torch.empty(3, H * Dk, cfg.short_conv, dtype=cfg.dtype))
        self.o_proj = QuantLinear(H * Dk, d, cfg.group)
        self.scale = Dk ** -0.5

    def _short_conv(self, val, prev, idx):
        win = torch.cat([prev, val[None]], dim=0)
        w = self.conv_w[idx].float().transpose(0, 1)
        out = (win.float() * w).sum(0)
        return F.silu(out).to(val.dtype), win[1:]

    def step(self, x, st):
        H, Dk = self.cfg.kda_heads, self.cfg.kda_head_dim
        q = self.q_proj(x)
        k = self.k_proj(x)
        v = self.v_proj(x)
        q, st["cq"] = self._short_conv(q, st["cq"], 0)
        k, st["ck"] = self._short_conv(k, st["ck"], 1)
        v, st["cv"] = self._short_conv(v, st["cv"], 2)
        q = q.view(H, Dk).float() * self.scale
        k = k.view(H, Dk).float()
        v = v.view(H, Dk).float()
        g = (-F.softplus(self.g_proj(x).float())).view(H, Dk)
        beta = torch.sigmoid(self.beta_proj(x).float())
        S = st["S"] * g.exp()[:, :, None]
        pred = (S * k[:, :, None]).sum(1)
        S = S + beta[:, None, None] * k[:, :, None] * (v - pred)[:, None, :]
        o = (S * q[:, :, None]).sum(1)
        st["S"] = S
        return self.o_proj(o.reshape(H * Dk).to(torch.bfloat16))


class MLA(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg: Config):
        super().__init__()
        self.cfg = cfg
        H, d = cfg.mla_heads, cfg.hidden
        self.q_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * (cfg.qk_nope + cfg.qk_rope), cfg.group)
        self.kv_a = QuantLinear(d, cfg.kv_lora + cfg.qk_rope, cfg.group)
        self.kv_b = QuantLinear(cfg.kv_lora, H * (cfg.qk_nope + cfg.v_head), cfg.group)
        self.o_proj = QuantLinear(H * cfg.v_head, d, cfg.group)
        self.scale = (cfg.qk_nope + cfg.qk_rope) ** -0.5

    def _warm_cache(self, st):
        """Project the pre-filled compressed latent cache to k_nope / v once."""
        if "k_nope" in st and "v" in st:
            return
        c_kv = st["c_kv"]
        L = c_kv.shape[0]
        H = self.cfg.mla_heads
        # Materialize kv_b for a single batched matmul at startup only.
        W = dequant(self.kv_b.w_q, self.kv_b.scales, self.kv_b.zeros, self.cfg.kv_lora, self.cfg.group)
        kvb = (c_kv.float() @ W.float()).view(L, H, self.cfg.qk_nope + self.cfg.v_head)
        st["k_nope"] = kvb[..., : self.cfg.qk_nope].to(self.cfg.dtype)
        st["v"] = kvb[..., self.cfg.qk_nope :].to(self.cfg.dtype)

    def step(self, x, st):
        cfg = self.cfg
        H = cfg.mla_heads
        pos = st["c_kv"].shape[0]
        q = self.q_proj(x).view(H, cfg.qk_nope + cfg.qk_rope)
        q_nope = q[:, : cfg.qk_nope].float()
        q_rope = q[:, cfg.qk_nope :]
        kv = self.kv_a(x)
        c_kv = kv[: cfg.kv_lora]
        k_rope = kv[cfg.kv_lora :]
        cos, sin = _rope_cossin(pos, cfg.qk_rope, cfg.rope_theta, x.device)
        q_rope = _apply_rope(q_rope, cos, sin).float()
        k_rope = _apply_rope(k_rope, cos, sin)

        self._warm_cache(st)

        # Project the new token's latent vector and append to the absorbed caches.
        kvb_new = self.kv_b(c_kv).view(H, cfg.qk_nope + cfg.v_head).float()
        k_nope_new = kvb_new[..., : cfg.qk_nope].to(cfg.dtype)
        v_new = kvb_new[..., cfg.qk_nope :].to(cfg.dtype)

        st["c_kv"] = torch.cat([st["c_kv"], c_kv[None]], 0)
        st["k_rope"] = torch.cat([st["k_rope"], k_rope[None]], 0)
        st["k_nope"] = torch.cat([st["k_nope"], k_nope_new[None]], 0)
        st["v"] = torch.cat([st["v"], v_new[None]], 0)

        scores = (torch.einsum("hd,lhd->lh", q_nope, st["k_nope"].float())
                  + torch.einsum("hd,ld->lh", q_rope, st["k_rope"].float())) * self.scale
        p = torch.softmax(scores, dim=0).to(x.dtype)
        o = torch.einsum("lh,lhd->hd", p, st["v"])
        return self.o_proj(o.reshape(H * cfg.v_head).to(torch.bfloat16))


class MoE(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg: Config):
        super().__init__()
        self.cfg = cfg
        d, m, E = cfg.hidden, cfg.moe_inter, cfg.n_experts
        self.router = nn.Linear(d, E, bias=False, dtype=cfg.dtype)
        self.gate = QuantExperts(E, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.up = QuantExperts(E, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.down = QuantExperts(E, m, d, cfg.group)
        self.s_gate = QuantExperts(cfg.n_shared, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.s_up = QuantExperts(cfg.n_shared, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.s_down = QuantExperts(cfg.n_shared, m, d, cfg.group)

    def step(self, x):
        cfg = self.cfg
        probs = torch.softmax(self.router(x).float(), dim=-1)
        w, idx = torch.topk(probs, cfg.n_active)
        w = w / (w.sum() + 1e-9) * cfg.routed_scaling
        routed_idx = idx.to(torch.int64)
        shared_idx = torch.arange(cfg.n_shared, device=x.device, dtype=torch.int64)

        gate_routed = self.gate.forward_batched(x, routed_idx)
        gate_shared = self.s_gate.forward_batched(x, shared_idx)
        gate_outs = torch.cat([gate_routed, gate_shared], dim=0)
        up_routed = self.up.forward_batched(x, routed_idx)
        up_shared = self.s_up.forward_batched(x, shared_idx)
        up_outs = torch.cat([up_routed, up_shared], dim=0)
        h = F.silu(gate_outs) * up_outs

        down_routed = self.down.forward_batched(h[: cfg.n_active], routed_idx)
        down_shared = self.s_down.forward_batched(h[cfg.n_active :], shared_idx)
        down_outs = torch.cat([down_routed, down_shared], dim=0)

        weights = torch.cat([w, torch.ones(cfg.n_shared, device=x.device, dtype=probs.dtype)])
        out = (weights[:, None].float() * down_outs.float()).sum(0)
        return out.to(torch.bfloat16)


class Block(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg: Config, kind: str):
        super().__init__()
        self.kind = kind
        self.attn_norm = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(cfg.hidden, dtype=cfg.dtype))
        self.moe_norm = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(cfg.hidden, dtype=cfg.dtype))
        self.attn = KDA(cfg) if kind == "K" else MLA(cfg)
        self.moe = MoE(cfg)

    def step(self, x, st):
        h = x + self.attn.step(_rmsnorm(x, self.attn_norm), st)
        return h + self.moe.step(_rmsnorm(h, self.moe_norm))


class Model(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg: Config):
        super().__init__()
        self.cfg = cfg
        self.blocks = nn.ModuleList(Block(cfg, k) for k in cfg.pattern)
        self.reset_parameters()

    def reset_parameters(self):
        g = torch.Generator(device="cpu").manual_seed(1234)
        for mod in self.modules():
            if isinstance(mod, (QuantLinear, QuantExperts)):
                mod.init_random(g)
            elif isinstance(mod, nn.Linear):
                nn.init.normal_(mod.weight, 0.0, 0.02, generator=g)
            elif isinstance(mod, KDA):
                nn.init.normal_(mod.conv_w, 0.0, 0.1, generator=g)

    def step(self, hidden, state):
        for i, blk in enumerate(self.blocks):
            hidden = blk.step(hidden, state[i])
        return hidden, state


# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
# State / inputs
# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
def init_state(cfg: Config, context_len: int, seed: int) -> list:
    dev = torch.device("cuda:0")
    g = torch.Generator(device=dev).manual_seed(seed)
    H, Dk = cfg.kda_heads, cfg.kda_head_dim
    C = H * Dk
    state = []
    for kind in cfg.pattern:
        if kind == "K":
            state.append({
                "S": torch.randn(H, Dk, Dk, device=dev, generator=g) * 0.05,
                "cq": torch.randn(cfg.short_conv - 1, C, device=dev, generator=g, dtype=cfg.dtype) * 0.1,
                "ck": torch.randn(cfg.short_conv - 1, C, device=dev, generator=g, dtype=cfg.dtype) * 0.1,
                "cv": torch.randn(cfg.short_conv - 1, C, device=dev, generator=g, dtype=cfg.dtype) * 0.1,
            })
        else:
            state.append({
                "c_kv": torch.randn(context_len, cfg.kv_lora, device=dev, generator=g, dtype=cfg.dtype) * 0.1,
                "k_rope": torch.randn(context_len, cfg.qk_rope, device=dev, generator=g, dtype=cfg.dtype) * 0.1,
            })
    return state


def init_token(cfg: Config, seed: int) -> torch.Tensor:
    dev = torch.device("cuda:0")
    g = torch.Generator(device=dev).manual_seed(seed + 1)
    return torch.randn(cfg.hidden, device=dev, generator=g, dtype=cfg.dtype) * 0.25

1	"""PyTorch reference for a Kimi-Linear W4A16 hybrid decode unit (batch=1).
2	
3	Correctness oracle, NOT the fast baseline (baseline.py) or the SOTA ceiling.
4	One repeating motif of Kimi-Linear-48B-A3B -- 3 KDA (gated-delta linear attn)
5	layers + 1 MLA (multi-head latent attention) layer, each + a 64-expert MoE FFN
6	-- decoded one token at a time, with the big projection weights stored as
7	**W4A16** (int4 weights, group-128 asymmetric, bf16 accumulation; the AWQ/GPTQ
8	format that open-source inference actually ships).
9	
10	Why W4A16 and not fp8: at batch-1 decode the bottleneck is *weight memory
11	traffic*. int4 weights are 0.25x the bytes of bf16 (4x less traffic), and a
12	fused dequant-GEMV realizes that win in the memory-bound regime where decode
13	lives -- unlike fp8 tensor-core matmul, which has fixed overhead and loses at
14	M=1. int4/bf16-acc also needs no special tensor-core format, so it runs on any
15	bf16-capable GPU (Ampere, Hopper, Blackwell).
16	
17	The two decode states are unchanged: KDA carries a fixed-size recurrent state
18	S[H,Dk,Dv] + short-conv window; MLA carries a growing compressed latent KV
19	cache. `step(hidden, state) -> (hidden, state)` consumes one token.
20	
21	This reference dequantizes naively (unpack -> bf16 matrix -> matmul). The whole
22	problem is to FUSE the int4 unpack+dequant into the GEMV and never materialize
23	the bf16 weight. Pack format is identical to KernelBench-Hard problem 07.
24	
25	Contract (reference.py / baselin

1	"""Latency benchmark for the Kimi-Linear hybrid decode unit.
2	
3	Score = baseline_latency / solution_latency (speedup over the optimized-PyTorch
4	baseline.py), geomean over the context-length sweep. The solution is timed
5	first; a final next-token check against the reference makes a fast-but-wrong
6	solution score zero. Absolute tok/s at the longest context is the shippable
7	"single-GPU decode" number.
8	
9	Reported in the peak_fraction field as a speedup multiple (>1 means faster than
10	the baseline), not a [0,1] roofline fraction.
11	"""
12	from __future__ import annotations
13	
14	import sys
15	import time
16	from math import exp, log
17	from pathlib import Path
18	
19	import torch
20	import yaml
21	
22	
23	def _run(model, cfg, ctx, steps, seed, ref):
24	    h = ref.init_token(cfg, seed)
25	    st = ref.init_state(cfg, ctx, seed)
26	    with torch.no_grad():
27	        for _ in range(steps):
28	            h, st = model.step(h, st)
29	    torch.cuda.synchronize()
30	    return h
31	
32	
33	def _time(model, cfg, ctx, steps, seed, ref):
34	    _run(model, cfg, ctx, min(3, steps), seed, ref)   # warmup
35	    torch.cuda.synchronize()
36	    best = float("inf")
37	    for _ in range(int(yaml.safe_load(Path("problem.yaml").read_text()).get("num_perf_trials", 3))):
38	        t0 = time.perf_counter()
39	        h = _run(model, cfg, ctx, steps, seed, ref)
40	        best = min(best, time.perf_counter() - t0)
41	    return best, h
42

We need implement solution.py with fused int4 dequant GEMV. Let's understand workload. Config: hidden 2304, KDA heads 32 dim128, short conv 4. MLA: heads32, kv_lora512, qk_nope128, qk_rope64, v_head128. MoE: 64 experts top8 +1 shared, intermediate 1024. Pattern K K K M. So per step: 3 KDA layers + MLA layer, each + MoE. So total layers: 4*(attn + MoE). But MoE is heavy: each layer has MoE with top8 experts + shared. Weights: - KDA q,k,v,g,o projections: q/k/v/g each 2304->4096 (32*128). o 4096->2304. Weight sizes in int4: q/k/v/g: w_q [1152,4096] uint8, scales [18,4096] bf16. o: [2048,2304] uint8? Wait in 4096/2=2048, scales 4096/128=32. - MLA q_proj: 2304 -> 32*(128+64)=6144. w_q [1152,6144]; kv_a: 2304 -> 512+64=576; kv_b: 512 -> 32*(128+128)=8192; o_proj: 32*128=4096 -> 2304. - MoE experts: gate/up/down for each expert. gate/up: d->m (2304->1024) each; down: m->d (1024->2304). 64 experts. Shared similar for n_shared=1. So total weight per layer huge: 4 KDA projections + 1 MLA q,kv_a,kv_b,o + MoE (8 selected out of 64 +1 shared). Since top8 selected per layer per token. Baseline dequantizes selected experts batched and matmuls. We need fused dequant-GEMV to avoid materializing bf16 weights. Also maybe for attention projections. Key challenge: implement fast custom GEMV fused with int4 unpack and per-group dequant. Options: 1. Triton kernel: each block handles a chunk of output channels, loads a contiguous stripe of int4 weight for all K, unpacks, dequantizes, accumulates dot product with x. For M=1, N output, K input. We want memory bandwidth bound: read int4 weights contiguously (K//2 bytes per output column) plus scales/zeros (K//128 * 2 bytes) and x (K bf16 ~ 2K bytes). To maximize bandwidth, one thread per output? Actually Triton GEMV with split K: each output element computed by reducing partial sums across K. Since weights are per-output column contiguous in K (weight shape K,N), each output can be computed independently by reading its own K column. That's efficient memory coalescing if each block/thread loads its column? However reading by column may be strided in memory: w_q shape (K//2, N), column-major contiguous along K if layout (K,N) row-major means columns are contiguous along K. So each output column data is contiguous K//2 bytes. Good. For bf16 x broadcast across N. We can compute y[n] = sum_k x[k] * dequant(w[k,n]). Triton kernel with one program per output column (or groups of columns). For N large (4096, 6144, 8192, 2304), launching N blocks fine. Each block loops over K in chunks of e.g. 128 (group size), unpacks two nibbles per byte, converts to bf16, dequant. Need accumulate in fp32. But for experts, we need multiple experts selected; can launch separate kernel per expert or batch. With top8 per MoE plus 1 shared per layer, 4 layers => 36 expert GEMVs per token? Each expert has gate, up, down. So 3 GEMVs per expert * 9 experts per layer * 4 layers = 108 GEMVs per token. Plus attention projections: per layer 5 GEMVs (q,k,v,g,o) for KDA x3 =15, MLA q,kv_a,kv_b,o=4 => total 19 attention GEMVs. Total ~127 GEMVs. Many small-ish. But each GEMV fusing unpack+dequant saves memory traffic. Alternatively, can write a single Triton kernel that handles batched weights for multiple experts? Maybe too complex. Let's first implement generic fused GEMV for all linears including experts. Need match state update exactly. Potential numerical differences: reference forward does x.float() @ weight_bf().float() -> bf16. Baseline uses bf16 matmul (x @ weight_bf). Fused kernel will compute in fp32 or bf16. Cosine similarity >=0.98 only, so some error acceptable. We should compute accumulate in fp32 for correctness. Important: State update uses bf16 for S? Actually reference S stored as float32? In init_state, S is torch.randn(...) no dtype -> default float32. q,k,v computed bf16 then .float(). S updated in fp32, stored fp32. MLA c_kv and k_rope bf16. We can keep same. +"""Kimi-Linear W4A16 hybrid decode unit — fused int4 dequant-GEMV.
+
+A from-scratch rewrite of reference.py that keeps the same module/state layout
+and numerical recipe, but does every weight-bound projection as a fused
+int4-unpack + per-group dequant + GEMV so the weights are streamed at int4
+bandwidth and never materialized as bf16.
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from dataclasses import dataclass, field
+
+import torch
+import torch.nn as nn
+import torch.nn.functional as F
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+OP_TYPE = "kimi_linear_w4a16_decode"
+HARDWARE_REQUIRED = ["RTX_PRO_6000"]
+EPS = 1.0e-6
+GROUP_SIZE = 128
+
+
+@dataclass(frozen=True)
+class Config:
+    hidden: int = 2304
+    kda_heads: int = 32
+    kda_head_dim: int = 128
+    short_conv: int = 4
+    mla_heads: int = 32
+    kv_lora: int = 512
+    qk_nope: int = 128
+    qk_rope: int = 64
+    v_head: int = 128
+    rope_theta: float = 10000.0
+    n_experts: int = 64
+    n_active: int = 8
+    n_shared: int = 1
+    moe_inter: int = 1024
+    routed_scaling: float = 2.446
+    group: int = 128
+    pattern: tuple = ("K", "K", "K", "M")
+    dtype: torch.dtype = field(default=torch.bfloat16)
+
+
+def build_config(shape: dict) -> Config:
+    return Config(n_experts=int(shape.get("n_experts", 64)))
+
+
+# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
+# Fused int4 GEMV kernel
+# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
+@triton.autotune(
+    configs=[
+        triton.Config({"BLOCK_N": 64, "GROUPS_PER_BLOCK": 1, "SPLIT_K": 1}, num_warps=4, num_stages=1),
+        triton.Config({"BLOCK_N": 128, "GROUPS_PER_BLOCK": 1, "SPLIT_K": 1}, num_warps=4, num_stages=1),
+        triton.Config({"BLOCK_N": 256, "GROUPS_PER_BLOCK": 1, "SPLIT_K": 1}, num_warps=8, num_stages=1),
+        triton.Config({"BLOCK_N": 128, "GROUPS_PER_BLOCK": 2, "SPLIT_K": 1}, num_warps=8, num_stages=1),
+        triton.Config({"BLOCK_N": 64, "GROUPS_PER_BLOCK": 2, "SPLIT_K": 1}, num_warps=4, num_stages=1),
+    ],
+    key=["K", "N"],
+)
+@triton.jit
+def int4_gemv_kernel(
+    x_ptr,
+    w_ptr,
+    s_ptr,
+    z_ptr,
+    y_ptr,
+    K,
+    N,
+    stride_wk,
+    stride_wn,
+    stride_sg,
+    stride_sn,
+    BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr,
+    GROUPS_PER_BLOCK: tl.constexpr,
+    SPLIT_K: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
+    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    mask_n = offs_n < N
+
+    # Each program optionally computes a partial sum for a subset of K tiles and
+    # reduces them.  For decode GEMV the K dimension is small enough that a
+    # single program over the full K is usually best, but keep the hook.
+    pid_k = tl.program_id(1) if SPLIT_K > 1 else 0
+    total_groups = (K + GROUP_SIZE - 1) // GROUP_SIZE
+    groups_per_split = (total_groups + SPLIT_K - 1) // SPLIT_K
+    g_start = pid_k * groups_per_split
+    g_end = tl.minimum((pid_k + 1) * groups_per_split, total_groups)
+
+    # Local buffer for the input slice being processed.  We load one logical
+    # group of x values (GROUP_SIZE floats) once and reuse it for every output
+    # channel in the tile.
+    x_buf = tl.zeros((GROUPS_PER_BLOCK * GROUP_SIZE,), dtype=tl.float32)
+
+    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), dtype=tl.float32)
+
+    g = g_start
+    while g < g_end:
+        gid = g
+        # How many real k-elements does this group cover?
+        g_k0 = gid * GROUP_SIZE
+        g_len = tl.minimum(GROUP_SIZE, K - g_k0)
+        gh = g_len // 2  # packed bytes in the group
+
+        # Load scale/zero for this group across the output tile.
+        scale = tl.load(
+            s_ptr + gid * stride_sg + offs_n * stride_sn,
+            mask=mask_n,
+            other=0.0,
+        ).to(tl.float32)
+        zero = tl.load(
+            z_ptr + gid * stride_sg + offs_n * stride_sn,
+            mask=mask_n,
+            other=0.0,
+        ).to(tl.float32)
+
+        # Load the input activations for this group once into registers.
+        for i in tl.static_range(0, GROUP_SIZE):
+            kidx = g_k0 + i
+            if i < g_len:
+                x_buf[i] = tl.load(x_ptr + kidx).to(tl.float32)
+
+        # Walk the packed bytes and unpack/dequant on the fly.
+        b0 = g_k0 // 2
+        for b in tl.range(0, gh):
+            k0 = g_k0 + 2 * b
+            byte = tl.load(
+                w_ptr + (b0 + b) * stride_wk + offs_n * stride_wn,
+                mask=mask_n,
+                other=0,
+            )
+            lo = (byte & 0xF).to(tl.float32)
+            hi = ((byte >> 4) & 0xF).to(tl.float32)
+            x0 = x_buf[2 * b]
+            x1 = x_buf[2 * b + 1]
+            acc += x0 * (lo - zero) * scale
+            acc += x1 * (hi - zero) * scale
+
+        g += GROUPS_PER_BLOCK
+
+    if SPLIT_K == 1:
+        tl.store(y_ptr + offs_n, acc.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask_n)
+    else:
+        # Atomic reduction across K splits.
+        tl.atomic_add(y_ptr + offs_n, acc, mask=mask_n)
+
+
+def fused_int4_gemv(x: torch.Tensor, w_q: torch.Tensor, scales: torch.Tensor, zeros: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    """M=1 GEMV: x @ W, where W is int4 packed + group-128 asymmetric dequant.
+
+    x:        [K] bf16 or fp16
+    w_q:      [K//2, N] uint8
+    scales:   [K//128, N] bf16
+    zeros:    [K//128, N] bf16
+    returns:  [N] bf16
+    """
+    assert x.dim() == 1
+    K, N = w_q.shape[0] * 2, w_q.shape[1]
+    y = torch.empty(N, dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
+    grid = lambda meta: (triton.cdiv(N, meta["BLOCK_N"]), meta["SPLIT_K"])
+    int4_gemv_kernel[grid](
+        x,
+        w_q,
+        scales,
+        zeros,
+        y,
+        K,
+        N,
+        w_q.stride(0),
+        w_q.stride(1),
+        scales.stride(0),
+

This condition is a scalar tensor? In Triton, comparison of dynamic scalar with constexpr returns a tensor scalar (0-d). The if statement may not be supported (Triton supports `if` on constexpr only? It supports runtime `if`? I think Triton allows `if` statements with scalar conditions in kernel, but it predicated execution. It might be okay but could be slow. Better to avoid by padding x with zeros and always loading full group, or load inside inner loop as scalar. Since group size 128, overhead of scalar load per byte inside inner loop already loads x. import torch, torch.nn.functional as F
import reference as R
import solution as S

cfg = R.build_config({'n_experts':64})
device='cuda'
ref = R.Model(cfg).to(device).eval()
sol = S.Model(cfg).to(device).eval()
sol.load_state_dict(ref.state_dict(), strict=True)
seed=0; ctx=2048
h = R.init_token(cfg, seed).clone()
st_ref = R.init_state(cfg, ctx, seed)
st_sol = S.init_state(cfg, ctx, seed)
with torch.no_grad():
    for i, (br, bs) in enumerate(zip(ref.blocks, sol.blocks)):
        o_r, st_ref = br.step(h.clone(), st_ref)
        o_s, st_sol = bs.step(h.clone(), st_sol)
        c = F.cosine_similarity(o_r.float().flatten(), o_s.float().flatten(), dim=0).item()
        print(f'block {i} ({br.kind}) out cos {c:.4f}')
        if br.kind=='K':
            print('  S cos', F.cosine_similarity(st_ref['S'].flatten(), st_sol['S'].flatten(), dim=0).item())
        else:
            print('  c_kv cos', F.cosine_similarity(st_ref['c_kv'].flatten(), st_sol['c_kv'].flatten(), dim=0).item())
            print('  k_rope cos', F.cosine_similarity(st_ref['k_rope'].flatten(), st_sol['k_rope'].flatten(), dim=0).item())
        h = o_r

import torch, torch.nn.functional as F
import reference as R
import solution as S

            print('  k_rope cos', F.cosine_similarity(st_ref[i]['k_rope'].flatten(), st_sol[i]['k_rope'].flatten(), dim=0).item())

import torch, torch.nn.functional as F
import reference as R
import solution as S

cfg=R.build_config({'n_experts':64})
ref=R.KDA(cfg).cuda().eval()
sol=S.KDA(cfg).cuda().eval()
sol.load_state_dict(ref.state_dict(), strict=True)
seed=0; ctx=2048
x = R.init_token(cfg, seed).clone()

with torch.no_grad():
    qr=ref.q_proj(x); qs=sol.q_proj(x)
    print('q_proj cos', F.cosine_similarity(qr.float(),qs.float(),dim=0).item(), 'max', (qr.float()-qs.float()).abs().max().item())
    qr, cqr = ref._short_conv(qr, st_r['cq'], 0)
    qs, cqs = sol._short_conv(qs, st_s['cq'], 0)
    print('q conv cos', F.cosine_similarity(qr.float(),qs.float(),dim=0).item())
    print('cq cos', F.cosine_similarity(cqr.float(),cqs.float(),dim=0).item())
    kr=ref.k_proj(x); ks=sol.k_proj(x)
    print('k_proj cos', F.cosine_similarity(kr.float(),ks.float(),dim=0).item(), 'max', (kr.float()-ks.float()).abs().max().item())
    kr, ckr = ref._short_conv(kr, st_r['ck'], 1)
    ks, cks = sol._short_conv(ks, st_s['ck'], 1)
    vr=ref.v_proj(x); vs=sol.v_proj(x)
    vr, cvr = ref._short_conv(vr, st_r['cv'], 2)
    vs, cks = sol._short_conv(vs, st_s['cv'], 2)
    gr=ref.g_proj(x); gs=sol.g_proj(x)
    print('g_proj cos', F.cosine_similarity(gr.float(),gs.float(),dim=0).item(), 'max', (gr.float()-gs.float()).abs().max().item())
    betar=torch.sigmoid(ref.beta_proj(x).float())
    betas=torch.sigmoid(sol.beta_proj(x).float())
    print('beta cos', F.cosine_similarity(betar.flatten(),betas.flatten(),dim=0).item(), 'max', (betar-betas).abs().max().item())

import torch, torch.nn.functional as F
import reference as R
import solution as S

cfg=R.build_config({'n_experts':64})
ref=R.Model(cfg).cuda().eval()
sol=S.Model(cfg).cuda().eval()
sol.load_state_dict(ref.state_dict(), strict=True)
seed=0; ctx=2048

    qr=ref_attn.q_proj(x); qs=sol_attn.q_proj(x)

    qs, cqs = sol_attn._short_conv(qs, st_s['cq'], 0)
    print('q conv cos', F.cosine_similarity(qr.float(),qs.float(),dim=0).item(), 'max', (qr.float()-qs.float()).abs().max().item())

    print('k_proj cos', F.cosine_similarity(kr.float(),ks.float(),dim=0).item(), 'max', (kr.float()-ks.float()).abs().max().item())

    print('g_proj cos', F.cosine_similarity(gr.float(),gs.float(),dim=0).item(), 'max', (gr.float()-gs.float()).abs().max().item())
    betar=torch.sigmoid(ref_attn.beta_proj(x).float())
    betas=torch.sigmoid(sol_attn.beta_proj(x).float())
    print('beta cos', F.cosine_similarity(betar.flatten(),betas.flatten(),dim=0).item(), 'max', (betar-betas).abs().max().item())
    or_ref=ref_attn.step(x.clone(), st_r)
    or_sol=sol_attn.step(x.clone(), st_s)
    print('out cos', F.cosine_similarity(or_ref.float(), or_sol.float(), dim=0).item(), 'max', (or_ref.float()-or_sol.float()).abs().max().item())

import torch, torch.nn.functional as F
import reference as R
import solution as S

cfg=R.build_config({'n_experts':64})
ref=R.Model(cfg).cuda().eval()
sol=S.Model(cfg).cuda().eval()

    o_r=ref_block.step(h0.clone(), st_r)
    o_s=sol_block.step(h0.clone(), st_s)

    as_=sol_block.attn.step(ns, st_s)

import torch, torch.nn.functional as F
import reference as R
import solution as S

cfg=R.build_config({'n_experts':64})
ref=R.Model(cfg).cuda().eval()
sol=S.Model(cfg).cuda().eval()
sol.load_state_dict(ref.state_dict(), strict=True)
seed=0; ctx=2048
h0=R.init_token(cfg, seed).clone()
ref_moe=ref.blocks[0].moe
sol_moe=sol.blocks[0].moe
with torch.no_grad():
    pr=F.softmax(ref_moe.router(h0).float(), dim=-1)
    ps=F.softmax(sol_moe.router(h0).float(), dim=-1)
    print('probs cos', F.cosine_similarity(pr, ps, dim=0).item(), 'max', (pr-ps).abs().max().item())
    wr, idxr = torch.topk(pr, cfg.n_active)
    ws, idxs = torch.topk(ps, cfg.n_active)
    print('idx same', (idxr==idxs).all().item())
    wrn = wr / (wr.sum()+1e-9) * cfg.routed_scaling
    wsn = ws / (ws.sum()+1e-9) * cfg.routed_scaling
    print('weights cos', F.cosine_similarity(wrn.float(), wsn.float(), dim=0).item(), 'max', (wrn-wsn).abs().max().item())
    # compare routed out per expert
    outr=torch.zeros(cfg.hidden, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    outs=torch.zeros(cfg.hidden, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    for j in range(cfg.n_active):
        er = ref_moe._ffn(h0, ref_moe.gate, ref_moe.up, ref_moe.down, int(idxr[j]))
        es = sol_moe._ffn(h0, int(idxs[j]))
        outr += wrn[j] * er
        outs += wsn[j] * es
    print('routed cos', F.cosine_similarity(outr, outs, dim=0).item(), 'max', (outr-outs).abs().max().item())

import torch, torch.nn.functional as F
import reference as R
import solution as S

cfg=R.build_config({'n_experts':64})
ref=R.Model(cfg).cuda().eval()
sol=S.Model(cfg).cuda().eval()
sol.load_state_dict(ref.state_dict(), strict=True)
seed=0; ctx=2048
h0=R.init_token(cfg, seed).clone()
ref_moe=ref.blocks[0].moe
sol_moe=sol.blocks[0].moe
with torch.no_grad():
    # routed manually like reference
    probs=F.softmax(ref_moe.router(h0).float(), dim=-1)
    w, idx = torch.topk(probs, cfg.n_active)
    w = w / (w.sum()+1e-9) * cfg.routed_scaling
    outr = torch.zeros(cfg.hidden, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    for j in range(cfg.n_active):
        outr += w[j] * ref_moe._ffn(h0, ref_moe.gate, ref_moe.up, ref_moe.down, int(idx[j]))
    for s in range(cfg.n_shared):
        outr += ref_moe._ffn(h0, ref_moe.s_gate, ref_moe.s_up, ref_moe.s_down, s)
    or_ref = outr.to(torch.bfloat16)

    probs_s=F.softmax(sol_moe.router(h0).float(), dim=-1)
    w_s, idx_s = torch.topk(probs_s, cfg.n_active)
    w_s = (w_s / (w_s.sum()+1e-9) * cfg.routed_scaling).to(h0.dtype)
    outs = torch.zeros(cfg.hidden, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    for j in range(cfg.n_active):
        outs += w_s[j] * sol_moe._ffn(h0, int(idx_s[j]))
    for s in range(cfg.n_shared):
        outs += sol_moe._ffn(h0, s)
    or_sol = outs.to(torch.bfloat16)
    print('moe manual cos', F.cosine_similarity(or_ref.float(), or_sol.float(), dim=0).item(), 'max', (or_ref.float()-or_sol.float()).abs().max().item())

import torch, torch.nn.functional as F
import reference as R
import solution as S

cfg=R.build_config({'n_experts':64})
ref=R.Model(cfg).cuda().eval()
sol=S.Model(cfg).cuda().eval()
sol.load_state_dict(ref.state_dict(), strict=True)
seed=0; ctx=2048

sol_moe=sol.blocks[0].moe

    outr = torch.zeros(cfg.hidden, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')

        shs += sol_moe._ffn(h0, s)

It loops K/2 up to 1152 iterations with dynamic `tl.range`, which may generate many instructions and poor occupancy. Also each iteration does two scalar loads from x (k0 and k0+1) and one vector load from weights. This is likely memory latency bound but also instruction overhead. We need a much faster kernel. Options: - Use vectorized unpack: load 4 bytes at once (uint32) and unpack 8 weights, compute dot product with x using tl.dot? But M=1. Could use `tl.sum` of vectorized multiply. - Or use `torch.compile` with custom dequant + matmul? But baseline uses bf16 matmul after dequant; to beat, need avoid materialization. - Use Triton GEMV with `tl.dot` on bf16/INT? We can dequant a tile to bf16 in shared memory and then use `tl.dot` with x tile. That would use tensor cores? For M=1, dot product of [1,K] and [K,N] with tl.dot would require x shape [BLOCK_K] and w shape [BLOCK_K,BLOCK_N], result [BLOCK_N]. tl.dot may be optimized. We can unpack a tile of int4 into bf16 in SMEM, then dot with x. But dequant in SMEM and dot could be faster. - Use `tl.interleave` for vectorized unpack. For each group, load packed bytes [BLOCK_K//2, BLOCK_N] uint8, unpack to [BLOCK_K,BLOCK_N] uint8, convert to bf16, subtract zero, multiply scale, then multiply by x[:,None] and accumulate via tl.sum or loop. Need be efficient. Maybe easier: since we have many small GEMVs, use `torch.compile` on a Python function that unpacks and dequant using vectorized PyTorch ops, then bf16 matmul. But baseline already does that. However baseline's `_batch_wbf` dequantizes selected experts batched and matmuls; for attention, baseline uses `_wbf` per step materializing weight (no batch). Our solution materializes no weights but per-byte kernel slower than PyTorch matmul because PyTorch matmul is highly optimized. To beat baseline, we need a near-optimal kernel. We need profile. Let's use ncu or torch.profiler. But first improve kernel. Observations: Baseline dequantizes all weights each step (for attention) and for experts selected. For attention weights (small), PyTorch matmul is fast. For experts, baseline batches 9 experts per linear type, so for gate: dequant 9 experts into [9,d,m] bf16, then matmul x[1,d] with batched weight? It uses `torch.einsum("e,kem->km", x, g)` where x shape [d], g shape [k=9,d,m]. This is essentially batched GEMV with dequantized weights. It's fast because uses cuBLAS batched GEMV and dequant uses vectorized PyTorch ops. Our per-byte Triton loop is slower. To beat baseline, we likely need to: 1. For attention projections, fuse int4 unpack but use efficient vectorized implementation, maybe competitive. 2. For MoE, batch the selected experts into a single kernel to reduce overhead and leverage coalescing. Alternative: Use `torch.compile` + `torch.mm` with a custom autograd? Not allowed prebuilt quantized kernel. But we can write dequant in PyTorch vectorized and use `torch.matmul` for batched experts; that's essentially baseline. To go faster, we must avoid writing dequantized bf16 weights to HBM. The memory bandwidth win is 4x, but baseline may be compute-bound in dequant? Actually baseline's bottleneck might be dequant+matmul reading/writing bf16 weights. Fused could win if kernel is efficient. Let's profile baseline and solution to see where time goes. Use `torch.profiler` for one step at ctx=8192. Or use nsight. Since GPU busy, profiling may be heavy. But let's use torch.profiler quickly. First, measure a single step latency (not full benchmark) for each layer type. Also try `torch.compile` on our model? But Triton kernels not compiled? Could wrap. Maybe we can use CUDA C++ extension for int4 GEMV with optimal memory access. But compile time. Triton should be enough. Let's inspect Triton kernel performance with vectorized unpack. import torch
import triton
import triton.language as tl

@triton.jit
def test_kernel(p, o, N):
    pid = tl.program_id(0)
    offs = pid + tl.arange(0,1)
    x = tl.load(p + pid)
    lo = x & 0xF
    hi = (x >> 4) & 0xF
    y = tl.interleave(lo, hi)
    tl.store(o + 2*pid + tl.arange(0,2), y)

p=torch.tensor([0x12, 0x34], dtype=torch.uint8, device='cuda')
o=torch.empty(4, dtype=torch.uint8, device='cuda')

import torch
import triton
import triton.language as tl

@triton.jit
def test_kernel(p, o, N):
    n = tl.arange(0, 2)
    x = tl.load(p + tl.arange(0,2)[:,None] * 2 + n[None,:])  # (2,2)
    lo = x & 0xF
    hi = (x >> 4) & 0xF
    # interleave along axis 0 via transposes
    y = tl.trans(tl.interleave(tl.trans(lo), tl.trans(hi)))
    tl.store(o + tl.arange(0,4)[:,None] * 2 + n[None,:], y)

p=torch.tensor([[0x12,0x34],[0x56,0x78]], dtype=torch.uint8, device='cuda')
o=torch.empty((4,2), dtype=torch.uint8, device='cuda')

     return y
 
 
+@triton.autotune(
+    configs=[
+        triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 64}, num_warps=4, num_stages=1),
+        triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 128}, num_warps=4, num_stages=1),
+        triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 256}, num_warps=8, num_stages=1),
+        triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 128}, num_warps=8, num_stages=1),
+    ],
+    key=["K", "N", "E"],
+)
+@triton.jit
+def int4_gemv_batched_kernel(
+    x_ptr,
+    w_ptr,
+    s_ptr,
+    z_ptr,
+    idx_ptr,
+    y_ptr,
+    K,
+    N,
+    E,
+    stride_we,
+    stride_wk,
+    stride_wn,
+    stride_se,
+    stride_sg,
+    stride_sn,
+    stride_ye,
+    stride_yn,
+    BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
+    BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
+    e = tl.load(idx_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
+    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    mask_n = offs_n < N
+
+    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), dtype=tl.float32)
+
+    num_blocks = (K + BLOCK_K - 1) // BLOCK_K
+    for b in tl.range(0, num_blocks):
+        k0 = b * BLOCK_K
+        offs_kh = k0 // 2 + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K // 2)
+        mask_kh = offs_kh < (K // 2)
+        w_pack = tl.load(
+            w_ptr + e * stride_we + offs_kh[:, None] * stride_wk + offs_n[None, :] * stride_wn,
+            mask=mask_kh[:, None] & mask_n[None, :],
+            other=0,
+        )
+        lo = w_pack & 0xF
+        hi = (w_pack >> 4) & 0xF
+        w_u = tl.trans(tl.interleave(tl.trans(lo), tl.trans(hi)))
+
+        g0 = k0 // 128
+        scale = tl.load(
+            s_ptr + e * stride_se + g0 * stride_sg + offs_n * stride_sn,
+            mask=mask_n,
+            other=0.0,
+        ).to(tl.float32)
+        zero = tl.load(
+            z_ptr + e * stride_se + g0 * stride_sg + offs_n * stride_sn,
+            mask=mask_n,
+            other=0.0,
+        ).to(tl.float32)
+
+        w_f = (w_u.to(tl.float32) - zero) * scale
+
+        offs_k = k0 + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+        mask_k = offs_k < K
+        x = tl.load(x_ptr + offs_k, mask=mask_k, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+
+        acc += tl.sum(w_f * x[:, None], axis=0)
+
+    tl.store(
+        y_ptr + pid_e * stride_ye + offs_n * stride_yn,
+        acc.to(tl.bfloat16),
+        mask=mask_n,
+    )
+
+
+def fused_int4_gemv_batched(
+    x: torch.Tensor,
+    w_q: torch.Tensor,
+    scales: torch.Tensor,
+    zeros: torch.Tensor,
+    idx: torch.Tensor,
+) -> torch.Tensor:
+    """Batched M=1 GEMV: for each selected expert i, compute x @ W[idx[i]].
+
+    x:        [K] bf16
+    w_q:      [E_total, K//2, N] uint8
+    scales:   [E_total, K//128, N] bf16
+    zeros:    [E_total, K//128, N] bf16
+    idx:      [E_sel] int64 (indices into w_q/scales/zeros)
+    returns:  [E_sel, N] bf16
+    """
+    assert x.dim() == 1
+    K = w_q.shape[1] * 2
+    N = w_q.shape[2]
+    E = idx.numel()
+    y = torch.empty((E, N), dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
+    grid = lambda meta: (E, triton.cdiv(N, meta["BLOCK_N"]))
+    int4_gemv_batched_kernel[grid](
+        x,
+        w_q,
+        scales,
+        zeros,
+        idx,
+        y,
+        K,
+        N,
+        E,
+        w_q.stride(0),
+        w_q.stride(1),
+        w_q.stride(2),
+        scales.stride(0),
+        scales.stride(1),
+        scales.stride(2),
+        y.stride(0),
+        y.stride(1),
+    )
+    return y
+
+

300	def dequant(w_q: torch.Tensor, scales: torch.Tensor, zeros: torch.Tensor, K: int, group: int) -> torch.Tensor:
301	    """Reference dequant (only used for one-time cache warmup)."""
302	    wu = torch.empty((K, w_q.shape[1]), dtype=torch.uint8, device=w_q.device)
303	    wu[0::2] = w_q & 0xF
304	    wu[1::2] = (w_q >> 4) & 0xF
305	    s = scales.repeat_interleave(group, dim=0)[:K]
306	    z = zeros.repeat_interleave(group, dim=0)[:K]
307	    return (wu.to(torch.bfloat16) - z) * s
308	
309	
310	class QuantLinear(nn.Module):
311	    def __init__(self, in_f: int, out_f: int, group: int = GROUP_SIZE):
312	        super().__init__()
313	        assert in_f % group == 0 and in_f % 2 == 0
314	        self.in_f, self.out_f, self.group = in_f, out_f, group
315	        ng = in_f // group
316	        self.register_buffer("w_q", torch.zeros(in_f // 2, out_f, dtype=torch.uint8))
317	        self.register_buffer("scales", torch.zeros(ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))
318	        self.register_buffer("zeros", torch.zeros(ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))
319	
320	    def init_random(self, gen: torch.Generator, std: float = 0.02) -> None:
321	        w = torch.randn(self.in_f, self.out_f, generator=gen) * std
322	        wq, s, z = quantize(w, self.group)
323	        self.w_q.copy_(wq)
324	        self.scales.copy_(s)
325	        self.zeros.copy_(z)
326	
327	    def forward(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
328	        return fused_int4_gemv(x, self.w_q, self.scales, self.zeros)
32

def int4_gemv_batched_kernel(
    x_ptr,
    w_ptr,
    s_ptr,
    z_ptr,
    idx_ptr,
    y_ptr,
    K,
    N,
    E,
    stride_we,
    stride_wk,
    stride_wn,
    stride_se,
    stride_sg,
    stride_sn,
    stride_ye,
    stride_yn,
    BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr,
):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    e = tl.load(idx_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    mask_n = offs_n < N

    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), dtype=tl.float32)

    num_blocks = (K + BLOCK_K - 1) // BLOCK_K
    for b in tl.range(0, num_blocks):
        k0 = b * BLOCK_K
        offs_kh = k0 // 2 + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K // 2)
        mask_kh = offs_kh < (K // 2)
        w_pack = tl.load(
            w_ptr + e * stride_we + offs_kh[:, None] * stride_wk + offs_n[None, :] * stride_wn,
            mask=mask_kh[:, None] & mask_n[None, :],
            other=0,
        )
        lo = w_pack & 0xF
        hi = (w_pack >> 4) & 0xF
        w_u = tl.trans(tl.interleave(tl.trans(lo), tl.trans(hi)))

        g0 = k0 // 128
        scale = tl.load(
            s_ptr + e * stride_se + g0 * stride_sg + offs_n * stride_sn,
            mask=mask_n,
            other=0.0,
        ).to(tl.float32)
        zero = tl.load(
            z_ptr + e * stride_se + g0 * stride_sg + offs_n * stride_sn,
            mask=mask_n,
            other=0.0,
        ).to(tl.float32)

def int4_gemv_batched_kernel(
    x_ptr,
    w_ptr,
    s_ptr,
    z_ptr,
    idx_ptr,
    y_ptr,
    K,
    N,
    E,
    stride_we,
    stride_wk,
    stride_wn,
    stride_se,
    stride_sg,
    stride_sn,
    stride_ye,
    stride_yn,
    BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr,
):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    e = tl.load(idx_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    mask_n = offs_n < N

    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), dtype=tl.float32)

    num_blocks = (K + BLOCK_K - 1) // BLOCK_K
    for b in tl.range(0, num_blocks):
        k0 = b * BLOCK_K
        offs_kh = k0 // 2 + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K // 2)
        mask_kh = offs_kh < (K // 2)
        w_pack = tl.load(
            w_ptr + e * stride_we + offs_kh[:, None] * stride_wk + offs_n[None, :] * stride_wn,
            mask=mask_kh[:, None] & mask_n[None, :],
            other=0,
        )
        lo = w_pack & 0xF
        hi = (w_pack >> 4) & 0xF
        w_u = tl.trans(tl.interleave(tl.trans(lo), tl.trans(hi)))

        g0 = k0 // 128
        scale = tl.load(
            s_ptr + e * stride_se + g0 * stride_sg + offs_n * stride_sn,
            mask=mask_n,
            other=0.0,
        ).to(tl.float32)
        zero = tl.load(
            z_ptr + e * stride_se + g0 * stride_sg + offs_n * stride_sn,
            mask=mask_n,
            other=0.0,
        ).to(tl.float32)

import re
path='/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/mega/outputs/runs/20260618_150545_kimi-claude_kimi-k2.7-code_03_kimi_linear_decode/repo/problems/03_kimi_linear_decode/solution.py'
src=open(path).read()

new_batched = '''@triton.autotune(
    configs=[
        triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 64}, num_warps=4, num_stages=1),
        triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 128}, num_warps=4, num_stages=1),
        triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 256}, num_warps=8, num_stages=1),
        triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 128}, num_warps=8, num_stages=1),
    ],
    key=["K", "N", "E"],
)
@triton.jit
def int4_gemv_batched_kernel(
    x_ptr,
    w_ptr,
    s_ptr,
    z_ptr,
    idx_ptr,
    y_ptr,
    K,
    N,
    E,
    stride_xe,
    stride_we,
    stride_wk,
    stride_wn,
    stride_se,
    stride_sg,
    stride_sn,
    stride_ye,
    stride_yn,
    BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr,
):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    e = tl.load(idx_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    mask_n = offs_n < N

    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), dtype=tl.float32)

    num_blocks = (K + BLOCK_K - 1) // BLOCK_K
    for b in tl.range(0, num_blocks):
        k0 = b * BLOCK_K
        offs_kh = k0 // 2 + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K // 2)
        mask_kh = offs_kh < (K // 2)
        w_pack = tl.load(
            w_ptr + e * stride_we + offs_kh[:, None] * stride_wk + offs_n[None, :] * stride_wn,
            mask=mask_kh[:, None] & mask_n[None, :],
            other=0,
        )
        lo = w_pack & 0xF
        hi = (w_pack >> 4) & 0xF
        w_u = tl.trans(tl.interleave(tl.trans(lo), tl.trans(hi)))

        g0 = k0 // 128
        scale = tl.load(
            s_ptr + e * stride_se + g0 * stride_sg + offs_n * stride_sn,
            mask=mask_n,
            other=0.0,
        ).to(tl.float32)
        zero = tl.load(
            z_ptr + e * stride_se + g0 * stride_sg + offs_n * stride_sn,
            mask=mask_n,
            other=0.0,
        ).to(tl.float32)

        w_f = (w_u.to(tl.float32) - zero) * scale

        offs_k = k0 + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
        mask_k = offs_k < K
        x = tl.load(x_ptr + pid_e * stride_xe + offs_k, mask=mask_k, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)

        acc += tl.sum(w_f * x[:, None], axis=0)

    tl.store(
        y_ptr + pid_e * stride_ye + offs_n * stride_yn,
        acc.to(tl.bfloat16),
        mask=mask_n,
    )


def fused_int4_gemv_batched(
    x: torch.Tensor,
    w_q: torch.Tensor,
    scales: torch.Tensor,
    zeros: torch.Tensor,
    idx: torch.Tensor,
) -> torch.Tensor:
    """Batched M=1 GEMV: for each selected expert i, compute x[i] @ W[idx[i]].

    x:        [K] or [E_sel, K] bf16
    w_q:      [E_total, K//2, N] uint8
    scales:   [E_total, K//128, N] bf16
    zeros:    [E_total, K//128, N] bf16
    idx:      [E_sel] int64 (indices into w_q/scales/zeros)
    returns:  [E_sel, N] bf16
    """
    E = idx.numel()
    if x.dim() == 1:
        x = x.unsqueeze(0).expand(E, -1).contiguous()
    assert x.dim() == 2 and x.shape[0] == E
    K = w_q.shape[1] * 2
    N = w_q.shape[2]
    y = torch.empty((E, N), dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
    grid = lambda meta: (E, triton.cdiv(N, meta["BLOCK_N"]))
    int4_gemv_batched_kernel[grid](
        x,
        w_q,
        scales,
        zeros,
        idx,
        y,
        K,
        N,
        E,
        x.stride(0),
        w_q.stride(0),
        w_q.stride(1),
        w_q.stride(2),
        scales.stride(0),
        scales.stride(1),
        scales.stride(2),
        y.stride(0),
        y.stride(1),
    )
    return y
'''

# replace from @triton.autotune(...key=["K","N","E"]) through return y of batched function

def fused_int4_gemv_batched(
    x: torch.Tensor,
    w_q: torch.Tensor,
    scales: torch.Tensor,
    zeros: torch.Tensor,
    idx: torch.Tensor,
) -> torch.Tensor:
    """Batched M=1 GEMV: for each selected expert i, compute x[i] @ W[idx[i]].

    x:        [K] or [E_sel, K] bf16
    w_q:      [E_total, K//2, N] uint8
    scales:   [E_total, K//128, N] bf16
    zeros:    [E_total, K//128, N] bf16
    idx:      [E_sel] int64 (indices into w_q/scales/zeros)
    returns:  [E_sel, N] bf16
    """
    E = idx.numel()
    if x.dim() == 1:
        x = x.unsqueeze(0).expand(E, -1).contiguous()
    assert x.dim() == 2 and x.shape[0] == E
    K = w_q.shape[1] * 2
    N = w_q.shape[2]
    y = torch.empty((E, N), dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
    grid = lambda meta: (E, triton.cdiv(N, meta["BLOCK_N"]))
    int4_gemv_batched_kernel[grid](
        x,
        w_q,
        scales,
        zeros,
        idx,
        y,
        K,
        N,
        E,
        x.stride(0),
        w_q.stride(0),
        w_q.stride(1),
        w_q.stride(2),
        scales.stride(0),
        scales.stride(1),
        scales.stride(2),
        y.stride(0),
        y.stride(1),
    )
    return y
'''

         triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 256}, num_warps=8, num_stages=1),
         triton.Config({"BLOCK_K": 128, "BLOCK_N": 128}, num_warps=8, num_stages=1),

 @triton.jit
-def int4_gemv_batched_kernel(+def int4_gemv_kernel(
+    x_ptr,
+    w_ptr,
+    s_ptr,
+    z_ptr,
+    y_ptr,
+    K,
+    N,
+    stride_wk,
+    stride_wn,
+    stride_sg,
+    stride_sn,
+    BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
+    BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
+    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    mask_n = offs_n < N
+
+    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), dtype=tl.float32)
+
+    num_blocks = (K + BLOCK_K - 1) // BLOCK_K
+    for b in tl.range(0, num_blocks):
+        k0 = b * BLOCK_K
+        offs_kh = k0 // 2 + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K // 2)
+        mask_kh = offs_kh < (K // 2)
+        w_pack = tl.load(
+            w_ptr + offs_kh[:, None] * stride_wk + offs_n[None, :] * stride_wn,
+            mask=mask_kh[:, None] & mask_n[None, :],
+            other=0,
+        )
+        lo = w_pack & 0xF
+        hi = (w_pack >> 4) & 0xF
+        w_u = tl.trans(tl.interleave(tl.trans(lo), tl.trans(hi)))
+
+        g0 = k0 // 128
+        scale = tl.load(
+            s_ptr + g0 * stride_sg + offs_n * stride_sn,
+            mask=mask_n,
+            other=0.0,
+        ).to(tl.float32)
+        zero = tl.load(
+            z_ptr + g0 * stride_sg + offs_n * stride_sn,
+            mask=mask_n,
+            other=0.0,
+        ).to(tl.float32)
+
+        w_f = (w_u.to(tl.float32) - zero) * scale
+
+        offs_k = k0 + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+        mask_k = offs_k < K
+        x = tl.load(x_ptr + offs_k, mask=mask_k, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+
+        acc += tl.sum(w_f * x[:, None], axis=0)
+
+    tl.store(y_ptr + offs_n, acc.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask_n)
+
+
+def fused_int4_gemv(x: torch.Tensor, w_q: torch.Tensor, scales: torch.Tensor, zeros: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    """M=1 GEMV: x @ W, where W is int4 packed + group-128 asymmetric dequant.
+
+    x:        [K] bf16 or fp16
+    w_q:      [K//2, N] uint8
+    scales:   [K//128, N] bf16
+    zeros:    [K//128, N] bf16
+    returns:  [N] bf16
+    """
+    assert x.dim() == 1
+    K, N = w_q.shape[0] * 2, w_q.shape[1]
+    y = torch.empty(N, dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
+    grid = lambda meta: (triton.cdiv(N, meta["BLOCK_N"]),)
+    int4_gemv_kernel[grid](
+        x,
+        w_q,
+        scales,
+        zeros,
+        y,
+        K,
+        N,
+        w_q.stride(0),
+        w_q.stride(1),
+        scales.stride(0),
+        scales.stride(1),
+    )
+    return y
+

reasoning (1415 chars)
For down batched, `h` shape [9,1024]. `routed_idx` length 8. `qe.forward_batched(inp, routed_idx)` expects x.shape[0]==E where E=8. But h shape[0]=9. We pass the same h to both routed and shared batched calls. We should split h into routed part (first 8 rows) and shared part (last row) matching indices. In `_batched`, we concatenated outputs from routed (8 rows) and shared (1 row). But input h is combined 9 rows; we need feed h[:8] to routed, h[8:] to shared. Let's adjust. Modify `_batched`: ``` def _batched(qe, s_qe, inp): routed = qe.forward_batched(inp[:cfg.n_active], routed_idx) shared = s_qe.forward_batched(inp[cfg.n_active:], shared_idx) return torch.cat([routed, shared], dim=0) ``` For gate/up, inp is 1D x. For x 1D, `inp[:cfg.n_active]` invalid (1D). So need handle: if inp.dim()==1, pass same to both; if 2D, split. Simpler: for gate/up, pass 1D; function expands. For down, pass h 2D and split. We can write two helpers or conditional. ``` def _batched_in(qe, s_qe, inp): return torch.cat([qe.forward_batched(inp, routed_idx), s_qe.forward_batched(inp, shared_idx)], dim=0) ``` For down, split manually: ``` down_routed = self.down.forward_batched(h[:cfg.n_active], routed_idx) down_shared = self.s_down.forward_batched(h[cfg.n_active:], shared_idx) down_outs = torch.cat([down_routed, down_shared], dim=0) ``` Similarly for gate/up use helper. Let's edit MoE.step accordingly.
